<script>
function getCookie(name) {
    var arg = name + "=";
    var alen = arg.length;
    var clen = document.cookie.length;
    var i = 0;
    while (i < clen) {
        var j = i + alen;
        if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg) {
            return getCookieVal(j);
        }
        i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
        if (i == 0) break;
    }
    return null;
}
function getCookieVal(offset) {
    var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf(";", offset);
    if (endstr == -1) {
        endstr = document.cookie.length;
    }
    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr));
}
function deleteCookie(name, path, domain) {
    if (getCookie(name)) {
        document.cookie = name + "=" +
            ((path) ? "; path=" + path : "") +
            ((domain) ? "; domain=" + domain : "") +
            "; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-70 00:00:01 GMT";
    }
}
function setCookie(name, value, expires, path, domain, secure) {
    document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) +
        ((expires) ? "; expires=" + expires : "") +
        ((path) ? "; path=" + path : "") +
        ((domain) ? "; domain=" + domain : "") +
        ((secure) ? "; secure" : "");
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
  (function() {
    var useSSL = 'https:' == document.location.protocol;
    var src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') +
        '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
    document.write('<scr' + 'ipt src="' + src + '" async></scr' + 'ipt>');

  var currentAdQueue = [];

    function infiniteAdController(section, pageNo, adQueue) {
        this.section = section;
        this.pageNo = pageNo;
        this.adQueue = adQueue;

        this.showAds = function(adQueue) {
            if (adQueue.length > 0) {
                for (i = 0; i < adQueue.length; i++) {
                    if (adQueue[i].skip == null) {
                        console.log(adQueue[i].key + ' Skip not provided.');
                        return;
                    }
                    if (adQueue[i].frequency == null) {
                        console.log(adQueue[i].key + ' Frequency not provided.');
                        return;
                    }

                    if ((adQueue[i].each != null)&&(pageNo - adQueue[i].skip)>=0) {
                        var array = adQueue[i].each.key.split('-');
                        for (j=0; j<array.length; j++){                                                  
                             if(pageNo%10 == array[j]){
                                ADTECH.loadAd(adQueue[i].key);  
                             }
                        }
                    }
                    else if (((pageNo - adQueue[i].skip) >= 0) && (pageNo - adQueue[i].skip) % adQueue[i].frequency == 0) {
                        ADTECH.loadAd(adQueue[i].key);
                    }
                }

            }
        }
    };


    function AdvPageChangeTrigger(section, pageno) {
        try {
            console.log('advpagechange=' + pageno);
            var adController = new infiniteAdController(section, pageno, currentAdQueue);
            adController.showAds(currentAdQueue);
        } catch (err) {}
    }
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        function GetSlickIndexForArticle() {
            var index = -1;
            var _hashValue = window.location.hash;
            if (_hashValue.indexOf("#a") == 0) {
                var _article = _hashValue.substring(2);
                var _image = $(".headlineNumeric.type01 img[data-id='" + _article + "']");
                index = _image.parents("li").index();
            }
            history.replaceState("", document.title, window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
            return index;
        }

        var currentItemFrontTop01 = GetSlickIndexForArticle();
        $('.headlineNumeric.type01 ul').on('init', function (event, slick) {
            $('.slick-dots li', slick.$slider.parent()).unbind('click');

            SlickInitialize(slick.$slider.parent(), 1);

            if (slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').hasClass('last-minute end'))
                slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current')
                    .find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/son-dakika.png" alt="" /></div>')
            else if (slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').hasClass('last-minute flash'))
                slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current')
                    .find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/flas-flas.png" alt="" /></div>')

            if (currentItemFrontTop01 > -1) {
                $('body').addClass('socialExtraMain') 
            }
        })
        .on('beforeChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {
            nextSlide == currentItemFrontTop01 ? $('body').addClass('socialExtraMain') : $('body').removeClass('socialExtraMain')
            if ($(slick.$slides[nextSlide]).hasClass('last-minute')) $(slick.$slides[nextSlide]).find('.slider-animation').remove();
        })
        .on('afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide) {
            var _image = $("img", slick.$slides[currentSlide]);
                 
            if ($(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).hasClass('last-minute end'))
                $(slick.$slides[currentSlide])
                    .find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/son-dakika.png" alt="" /></div>');
            else if ($(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).hasClass('last-minute flash'))
                $(slick.$slides[currentSlide])
                    .find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/flas-flas.png" alt="" /></div>');
        })
        .slick({
            dots: true,
            speed: 300,
            arrows: false,
            pauseOnDotsHover: true,
            customPaging: function (slider, i) {
                var _link = $('a', slider.$slides[i]).attr('href');
                return '<a target="_blank" href="' + _link + '">' + (i + 1) + '</a>';
            },
            initialSlide: (currentItemFrontTop01 < 0 ? 0 : currentItemFrontTop01)
        });
    </script>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                    /* ========[ manset slider numeric type 03 ]============ */
                    var _sliderheadlineNumeric03 = $('.headlineNumeric.type03 ul')
                        .on('init', function (event, slick) {
                            $('.slick-dots li', slick.$slider.parent()).unbind('click');

                            SlickInitialize(slick.$slider.parent(), 1);

                            if ( slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').hasClass('last-minute end') ) slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/son-dakika.png" alt="" /></div>')
                            else if (slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').hasClass('last-minute flash')) slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/flas-flas.png" alt="" /></div>')

                        })
                        .on('beforeChange', function(event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide){
                            var _image = $("img[src='" + _lazyLoadImage + "']", slick.$slides[nextSlide]);

                            $(_image).lazyload();
                            $(_image).trigger("appear");
                            if (slick.$slides.length >= nextSlide + 1) {
                                $("img", slick.$slides[nextSlide + 1]).lazyload();
                                $("img", slick.$slides[nextSlide + 1]).trigger("appear");
                            }

                            if ( $(slick.$slides[nextSlide]).hasClass('last-minute') ) $(slick.$slides[nextSlide]).find('.slider-animation').remove();

                        })
                        .on('afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide) {

                            if ($(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).hasClass('last-minute end')) $(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/son-dakika.png" alt="" /></div>');
                            else if ($(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).hasClass('last-minute flash')) $(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="http://i.sabah.com.tr/sbh/v6/i/flas-flas.png" alt="" /></div>');

                        })
                        .slick({
                            dots: true,
                            speed: 300,
                            arrows: true,
                            pauseOnDotsHover: true,
                            prevArrow: '<span class="slick-prev"><i class="fa fa-chevron-left" aria-hidden="true"></i></span>',
                            nextArrow: '<span class="slick-next"><i class="fa fa-chevron-right" aria-hidden="true"></i></span>',
                            customPaging: function (slider, i) {
                                var _link = $('a', slider.$slides[i]).attr('href');
                                return '<a target="_blank" href="' + _link + '">' + (i + 1) + '</a>';
                            }
                        });
                </script>

<script>
    $(function () {
        $.getJSON({
            url: "/json/mostviewedarticles",
            data: { categorynameforurl: "anasayfa" },
            type: "GET",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success) {
                    $("div.mostReadList div.row.row-flex.rule-align-between").hide();

                    var len = result.List.length;
                    $.each(result.List, function (index, item) {
                        var _singleItem = $("div.mostReadList div.col-sm-12.col-flex").first().clone();
                        if (len == index + 1)
                            _singleItem.removeClass("view20");

                        $("figure > a", _singleItem).attr("href", item.Url);

                        if ($("figure > a img", _singleItem).attr("data-original") !== undefined)
                            $("figure > a img", _singleItem).attr("data-original", item.Path);
                        else
                            $("figure > a img", _singleItem).attr("src", item.Path);

                        $("figure > a img", _singleItem).attr("alt", item.TitleShort);

                        $("figcaption > a", _singleItem).attr("href", item.Url)
                                                        .html(item.TitleShort);

                        $("div.mostReadList div.row.row-flex.rule-align-between").append(_singleItem);
                    });

                    $("div.mostReadList div.col-sm-12.col-flex").first().remove();

                    $("div.mostReadList div.row.row-flex.rule-align-between").show();
                    $("#divMostViewedArticles").show();
                    base.SetLazyLoad();
                }
            }
        });
    });  
</script>
            </div>

<script> 
    $(function () {
        var $ItemA, ts1A, ts2A, tabCtrlA = true;
        var exTabIndexA = 0;
        $('.sariSayfalar ul.tabs').find('li').each(function (index) {
            $(this).click(function () {
                if (tabCtrlA && exTabIndexA != index) {
                    tabCtrlA = false;
                    if (exTabIndexA == 0) { ts1A = 0; ts2A = 1 }
                    else if (exTabIndexA == 1) {
                        if (index == 0) { ts1A = 1; ts2A = 0 }
                        else { ts1A = 0; ts2A = 1 }
                    }
                    else if (exTabIndexA == 2) { ts1A = 1; ts2A = 0 }
                    $('.sariSayfalar ul.tabs').find('li').removeClass('current');
                    $(this).addClass('current');
                    $('.sariSayfalar .cells .cell').hide();
                    $('.sariSayfalar .cells .cell').eq(index).fadeIn();
                    tabCtrlA = true;
                    exTabIndexA = index;
                    base.SetLazyLoad();
                }
            });
        });
    }); 
</script>

}
